  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_833c8288-40aa-49ce-9a8e-ef3a5d3d4da8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer4495697447757272358">Beauty resents being labeled Gift Species. Everyone is way too overprotective, males aren’t even allowed to speak to her and so far true freedom eludes her. Then a big, sexy Species officer mistakes her for the enemy and takes her to the ground. <br/><br/>Shadow is dumbfounded. He has a Gift pinned under him—a big no-no. But Beauty is fascinated and wants to know Shadow a lot better</span>
  <span id="freeText4495697447757272358" style="display:none">Beauty resents being labeled Gift Species. Everyone is way too overprotective, males aren’t even allowed to speak to her and so far true freedom eludes her. Then a big, sexy Species officer mistakes her for the enemy and takes her to the ground. <br /><br />Shadow is dumbfounded. He has a Gift pinned under him—a big no-no. But Beauty is fascinated and wants to know Shadow a lot better. She is full of newly discovered, unrequited passion and he’s just what she needs to satisfy her curiosity. <br /><br />For Shadow, sex means pain and revulsion. For Beauty, it was enslavement and ridicule. Two lonely souls who have never known a lover’s touch, together in a cabin in the woods. Each touch, every discovery brings them closer to a life they never thought possible…beyond even their dreams.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8852485401613018757"><b> 4 I just had sex Stars</b><br/><br/><b>*Spoilers*</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/cCHvKpj_zps7uhfqosv.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

I have enough regrets.”</b><br/><br/><br/>So Shadow is the 9th book in the New Species Series. Beauty is sick of being called gift. Everyone treats her with kid gloves. Men aren't allowed to even talk to gift females. It's like a prettier prison, and Beauty is sick of it. She wants a life, love, and she just wants to be treated normal. One night while runnin</span>
  <span id="freeText8852485401613018757" style="display:none"><b> 4 I just had sex Stars</b><br><br><b>*Spoilers*</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/cCHvKpj_zps7uhfqosv.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1425325239ra/13877356.gif" alt=" photo cCHvKpj_zps7uhfqosv.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br><b>“I’m really not. I’m scared all the time but I’m more afraid of wasting the life I’ve been given by never taking chances. I have enough regrets.”</b><br><br><br>So Shadow is the 9th book in the New Species Series. Beauty is sick of being called gift. Everyone treats her with kid gloves. Men aren't allowed to even talk to gift females. It's like a prettier prison, and Beauty is sick of it. She wants a life, love, and she just wants to be treated normal. One night while running in the rain to feel free and alive, she is tackled by a NS male. She isn't afraid of him. She feels drawn to him. He is so big and sexy. She is going to have him and a life. Now she just has to figure out how to go about getting what she wants, when everyone treats her like a child!<br><br><b>“That’s what Gifts are to all of you, right? Children? Why did you bother to save us? It’s a prison without abuse but it’s still captivity. Sunshine, nicer living conditions, and food aren’t enough.”</b><br><br>Shadow:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/images%2017_zpsrpfxyqlh.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425325310i/13877372.jpg" alt=" photo images 17_zpsrpfxyqlh.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Shadow is messed up. While imprisoned he was hooked to a masterbation machine and forced to watch porn while they stole his semen to sell to people who wanted to make species babies for pets. He is afraid to touch a woman , doesn't know how he will act if he has flash backs. Then he meets Beauty and he has never wanted a female more. Shadow was sweet, sexy, and very protective.... I loved how he was always dropping to his knees to talk to her so they were eye level. He opened himself up to her made himself vulnerable . <br><br><br><b>“It means you shouldn’t say that to me unless you really mean it. I’d keep you in my bed, Beauty. You don’t need to worry about me with other females. I already avoid them. You’re the only one who tempts me to the point where I’d face anything to touch you.”<br><br><br><br>“I was afraid I might hurt you but I’ve wanted you since the moment we met.” He hugged her tighter to him. “I’m damaged and was worried that would cripple me when it came to sharing sex.” His fingers stroked her arm, glad she relaxed. “There isn’t a damn thing pathetic or lacking in you, Beauty.”<br><br><br><br>“I want to. I need to taste you. I crave it.” He took a heavy, shuddering breath. “Open up for me and stop thinking. Just feel. Trust me, Beauty.”</b><br><br><br>Beauty:<br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Dark-Brown-Long-Hairstyles-for-Women_zpss5iazfcx.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br>I loved Beauty she was so brave. She was scared but she wasn't going to let that hold her back. She knew what she wanted and went for it. She was a fighter and I loved that. I’m getting stronger every day and I refuse to be locked inside a box while you and everyone else toss away the key. I might not be as physically fit as our women but that doesn’t make me less.” <br><br><br>“You’re smaller than me and I worry I’d be too rough if I put my hands on you.” “You’re touching me right now and you’re being very gentle.” She swallowed hard. “Maybe we could help each other get over our pasts.”<br><br><br>“I’m not them, you know.” She swallowed. “I don’t want to have different sexual partners. I’m not opposed to dating you.” Her gaze dropped to his chest and stayed there, her embarrassment showing again in her cheeks. “That is, if you want to try out being my boyfriend. I’d prefer to have a monogamous relationship.”</b><br><br><br>I loved them as couple . They were strong for each other , being the others support. They were sugary sweet! I loved breeze in this book too. I want her to get her own book so bad. I enjoyed the plot in this one, liked the fact that it was her master that was the bad guy. Laughed so much over the way everyone was all up in their sex life, and when they had sex I was waiting for them to get a Hallmark card! <br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/510888_zpsj6kuci3w.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><b>“I love sex,” she admitted, obviously content to lie there with him curved around her. “I love sex with you,” he panted, brushing another kiss on her throat. “Was I too rough?” He worried he might inadvertently harm her frailer body.</b><br><br>I loved this book, it was another great one for the New Species Series. I am on to Moon!! Below I leave my favorite moment from the book:<br><br><br><b>“Why do you call Shadow that?” “Toga boy? It annoys him. Plus,” she laughed, “I’ll never forget what he looked like wearing that flag. It was kind of hot.” Jealousy surged inside Beauty. “He’s mine.” Dark eyebrows rose and Breeze grinned. “Feeling possessive? You just hissed at me.” “I’m sorry.” Beauty was surprised by her unexpected strong reaction. “He’s all yours. I can look but won’t touch. All our males are impressive, if I say so myself, and I do. Is he feeling possessive of you as well?” She grinned. “Never mind. He will. It’s who they are.”“I feel things for him.” “How is the sex?” Beauty hesitated but then answered. “Amazing!” She blushed but refused to look away. “It’s so much better than I ever suspected.” “Score points for toga boy!” Breeze chuckled. “I’m glad.” “Please don’t call him that. You have to notice how that muscle in his jaw twitches every time you say it.” “I know. It’s cute, isn’t it?” Breeze stood. “It’s good for males to be teased. It reminds them not to be serious all the time. What do you have to eat around here?”</b><br><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsession.blogspot.com/">http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsessio...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer231121436791374102">Well, I don't know about everyone else, but I loved this book. Beauty was awesome- the right blend of quiet and strength. And for some reason, I don't know why, I have discovered an obsession for Leo. I really don't know why, since he is only mentioned about three times in this book, but I adore him. He is mine, do you hear me? He. Is. Mine.<br/><i> Valiant has warned them sternly to avoid this area. He keeps them in control for the most part. Leo is also good with intimidation. He’s a wild bastard thou</i></span>
  <span id="freeText231121436791374102" style="display:none">Well, I don't know about everyone else, but I loved this book. Beauty was awesome- the right blend of quiet and strength. And for some reason, I don't know why, I have discovered an obsession for Leo. I really don't know why, since he is only mentioned about three times in this book, but I adore him. He is mine, do you hear me? He. Is. Mine.<br /><i> Valiant has warned them sternly to avoid this area. He keeps them in control for the most part. Leo is also good with intimidation. He’s a wild bastard though.”<br />“Who is Leo? Is he a danger?”<br />“Another feline. He won’t come after the Gift. I’d worry more about him playing pranks but he’s got heart. He’s sane but doesn’t follow rules. He enjoys giving the officers headaches.”</i><br />Ok, and maybe its the fact he has a tail. How cool is that? We finally have a species with a tail. Almost like Valiant, but not quite as crazy. And he's single! Or was- mine now...<br /><br />It definitely took some surprising turns for me, but I really enjoyed it. Beauty was quite lucky with the man she was gifted to, so I understand she was not quite like Tiny or Half-pint which is disappointing because I really enjoyed reading about a Gift female. Doesn't seem likely Tiny and Half-pint will get a book :( Maybe a different Gift female? Though I don't think we've heard of may others. Maybe a Gift with a Task force guy? That'd be a cool twist :D<br /><br />I was slightly happy that Moon's book was next [loved him ever since Slade] but I thought it wouldn't be as intense as the others because of how relaxed he is. Hah, well that's all ruined now. Can't wait for his book. Being shot with a dart that practically turns them feral? Didn't see that one coming. Moon promises to be interesting. <br /><br />Perhaps after Moon she will do Ven. I hope so, his story seems like it will be very interesting. Then Jericho? I really want to read his book too. I'd also want her to do Leo- but that would mean giving him up to a Species or human and there is no way I'm doing that.<br /><br />Why is it when I finally decide to hate someone in her books she makes them seem not that bad? Looks like there is a lot more to Kit than we thought. Someone has some hidden issues. But she's still not well liked by me- Obsidian is my second favorite male and he was <i>clearly</i> taken when she hit on him. Ven was annoying until we learned his story. Kit's story might be really sad, but she's still a bit of a bitch. Gonna have to work hard LD to make me like her.<br /><br />Moon can't come out fast enough. No release date for it yet- damn. Soon hopefully. I'm dying to see how and who solves the drug problem. I thought a doctor at first, but probably not. The girls are already taken, right? Trisha and Ali. Maybe a Species? Maybe a human? Who knows? It will have to come put quickly so when can find out- and get our next NS hit *hint hint*</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer245429107954382897">Ooo, this guy's name is Shadow. That makes me think of a mysterious dark-haired man who is a brooding and quiet. Like this:<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457855951i/18413360.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>But, that is completely wrong. Our guy named Shadow is tan, blonde hair in a military cut, blue eyes, easy-going and funny. Like a bro, not a shadow.<br/><br/>It just seems kinda deceiving. But, these New Species pick out some weird names sometimes. There is one named "Book", one named "Creek", and another named "Moon". I mean, I get that they all picked things they like but come on! </span>
  <span id="freeText245429107954382897" style="display:none">Ooo, this guy's name is Shadow. That makes me think of a mysterious dark-haired man who is a brooding and quiet. Like this:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457855951i/18413360.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But, that is completely wrong. Our guy named Shadow is tan, blonde hair in a military cut, blue eyes, easy-going and funny. Like a bro, not a shadow.<br><br>It just seems kinda deceiving. But, these New Species pick out some weird names sometimes. There is one named "Book", one named "Creek", and another named "Moon". I mean, I get that they all picked things they like but come on! If we were going to name ourselves random items we like, I would be called "Cake" or "Bed". Most of my dreams are cake related...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457855951i/18413361._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>A cake-bed - the best of both worlds!<br><br>So, we have Shadow, our bro New Species, doing guard duty at the compound one night when he spots Beauty, one of the female Species who had been used as a sex slave before being rescued. She is out running in a storm and he ends up taking shelter with her. The thing is, the males are not allowed to touch or even talk to the females that were rescued from sexual slavery. They are completely taboo - off limits - no-go zone. So, we all know what that means, right?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457855951i/18413362.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>No, it's "bow chicka wow wow", not brown chicken brown cow!<br><br>Beauty doesn't like being coddled and having no male exposure. She's lonely and she needs a little shadow in her life (and she needs a lotta Shadow in her bed), so she tells another female that she's ready for some action. They need to stop the cock-blocking!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457855951i/18413363._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>These New Species are very literal.<br><br>So, the New Species government does what all governments do: they have a meeting to discuss whether or not they will allow Beauty to have sex. Kinda reminds me of some old white guys who form special committees in the government to make decisions about women's reproductive issues. Oh, I'm not bitter or anything! If anyone could understand the complicated journey of a female navigating her sexuality and fertility, it's a group of old men in government.<br><br>Luckily for Beauty and Shadow, they vote to allow them to have sex. Thank goodness! If there had just been one vote swinging the other way, they might have had to stay away from each other for ever. Cuz, we all know that if the government told us that we can't have sex, we would all cease and desist immediately.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457855951i/18413364.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, they go to a cabin in the woods for some "alone time". There is some drama, but most of the book is them discussing their feelings. *sigh* I don't even like to discuss my own feelings, let alone read about other people's feeling discussions.<br><br>The only thing that saved this story for me was an awesome shoot-out in the woods, and Breeze who is by far one of the best characters in this series.</span>

Her guards referred to her as Mud. But she was a Gift. Gifts were New species that were genetically altered with animal DNA. They were developed to be sexual companions and they are beautiful. Beauty was created with Primate DNA.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380396408i/764084._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="536" alt="beauty standing" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The Gifts that have been rescued are treated like fine china. They are not allowed to interact with any males and not are not even allowed to work as all other New Species do. Beauty often hears the other species having sex thru the walls of her dorm, but instead of fear, she feels a longing. He has never had consensual sex and is afraid to attempt to be with a female. But Beauty is a temptation that he is unable to refuse. These two were so perfect for each other!<br><b>
  <blockquote>She’d wanted him to kiss her. Her head tilting back and her lips parting while she’d closed her eyes had been a good indication. There was only one problem. He’d never kissed a female before.</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380396408ra/764088.gif" width="400" height="192" alt="Beauty and Shadow" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I’ve never loved before but this has to be it. You are everything I want and need. You make me complete and having you in my arms is the most right thing in my world. Every thought involves you and how to keep you close.”</blockquote>
</b><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer13410057135801210760">I loved this one! I wasn't quite sure how I was going to feel about the pairing with Shadow & Beauty, but I must say these two are just beautiful together. I loved that this one is about a Species Female pairing this time and not our past books in this series where they are all about the Species Males & human females.<br/><br/><b>"What do you need? Tell me. It's yours." -Shadow</b> *sighs*<br/><a href='http://s1135.photobucket.com/albums/m630/Enhya77/?action=view&current=bfgw2w.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>Just because Beauty is alot more vulnerable than her female species counterparts, does in no way cancel out her ability t</span>
  <span id="freeText13410057135801210760" style="display:none">I loved this one! I wasn't quite sure how I was going to feel about the pairing with Shadow &amp; Beauty, but I must say these two are just beautiful together. I loved that this one is about a Species Female pairing this time and not our past books in this series where they are all about the Species Males &amp; human females.<br><br><b>"What do you need? Tell me. It's yours." -Shadow</b> *sighs*<br><a href="http://s1135.photobucket.com/albums/m630/Enhya77/?action=view&amp;current=bfgw2w.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Just because Beauty is alot more vulnerable than her female species counterparts, does in no way cancel out her ability to think, feel, and defend herself. She has heart. And she shows it beautifully.<br><br>I really love the message in this one: Just because one has endured unspeakable acts by the hands of another, does not mean one should remain in fear of living and loving. Taking back your power through living your life and moving forward in a positive way.<br><br>I like how this story was executed. The writing, and dialogue is definitely alot tighter in this one. I loved the brief glimpses we get from some of our previous Species males, and I just can't say this enough.. I love love love Shadow.<br><br>The heartfelt exchange you will see between Beauty and Shane towards the end was really beautiful. I'm glad I got to see that. I was wondering/hoping if or when we would ever see him again after meeting him in the prologue.<br><br>All in all this was another great installment to this series. I would recommend this read<br><br> ****Please read this series in order****</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4303933719412434637">**re-read after another re-read I think I would rate this a 4 now. I don't know how Beauty felt with everyone treating her like a kid, that would have driven me mad. <br/>Bumping this up to a 3 1/2 star rating, I still like this book but I still feel the same as the first time I read this one<br/>This is a hard review for me because I love Laurann Dohner I love her stories I love her style of writing and I always get wrapped into her worlds and her characters. But I knew from the beginning that I didn't r</span>
  <span id="freeText4303933719412434637" style="display:none">**re-read after another re-read I think I would rate this a 4 now. I don't know how Beauty felt with everyone treating her like a kid, that would have driven me mad. <br />Bumping this up to a 3 1/2 star rating, I still like this book but I still feel the same as the first time I read this one<br />This is a hard review for me because I love Laurann Dohner I love her stories I love her style of writing and I always get wrapped into her worlds and her characters. But I knew from the beginning that I didn't really want to read this book and it's nothing to do with her stories or her writing style I just have never been interested in reading about a "gift species", and that's why I waited so long to read this book. With Moon coming out in a few days(YAY!) I knew I needed to get down to it and read this book. Even though I wasn't interested in a gift female I have to say that LD still brought a really good story, the world building was great and the incorporation of the side characters were great. <br /><br />This book was a lot different than the other books in that we don't get a lot of external problems. This book focuses almost completely on Shadow and beauty and them being together the whole time. It was interesting to see how the gift females were treated, and that while the species were trying their best to protect the gift females they were actually giving them a pretty prisons and treating them like kids. After reading this book I dislike Kit more and as always Breeze was great. So yes the story was good but I couldn't connect with the heroine and didn't like it as much as the others.</span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14108764-malinda?shelf=job-men-in-uniform">job-men-in-uniform</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722516339" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5214641116458096892">4-4.5 stars<br/><br/>This was a really good story. I loved Beauty and Shadow and really enjoyed their story. This one has made it to my second favorite of this series (I can't help it, Valiant is still my fave). <br/><br/>Beauty is a NS (New Species - people that were made in a lab with human DNA merged with animal DNA) female but also has the misfortune of being a "Gift" female (the NS females that were made smaller and weaker than most NS and given away to the financiers of the lab that created them). This meant </span>
  <span id="freeText5214641116458096892" style="display:none">4-4.5 stars<br /><br />This was a really good story. I loved Beauty and Shadow and really enjoyed their story. This one has made it to my second favorite of this series (I can't help it, Valiant is still my fave). <br /><br />Beauty is a NS (New Species - people that were made in a lab with human DNA merged with animal DNA) female but also has the misfortune of being a "Gift" female (the NS females that were made smaller and weaker than most NS and given away to the financiers of the lab that created them). This meant she was put through some really bad stuff by a man that saw her as a possession. Fortunately for Beauty, she was rescued and taken to Homeland (a compound owned by the freed NS people) where she recovered and learned to live free. The problem is that since the "Gift" females as seen as weak, they're highly protected. The NS males aren't even allowed to talk to them and their movements (even within the compound) are very restricted. Most of the "Gift" females don't mind because they have no interest in males but Beauty is different. Beauty is trying to get over her past abuse and wants a relationship with a male. Kind of hard to do when you're not even allowed to talk to them. One night when she's feeling very restrained by her circumstances, she leaves the women's dorms and goes for a run, not expecting to get tackled when she's mistaken for a human. <br /><br />Shadow is a NS male and has been through a rough past in the labs which has him avoiding females (intimately). He has been working with the human task force that goes out to capture the fugitives still out there wanted for crimes against the NS people and also saving any NS people that discovered being held captive. He's best friends with Wrath and envies him his mate but doubts he'll ever be able to want a female (human or NS) or ever have a mate. Things change when he captures what he thinks is a human intruder in Homeland and she ends up being a "Gift" NS female instead. <br /><br />When Shadow captures Beauty, there's a bad storm that comes up and as he's trying to get her protection from the rain, he takes them to a storage shed in the area. As soon as they get inside, hail starts up and it's too dangerous to go outside for a while. When it's safer, Shadow wants to go call a female NS officer (standard procedure with a "Gift" female) but Beauty doesn't want him to leave. She's interested in the big NS male and convinces him she'd be too scared if he left her alone (a bit of an exaggeration) so he wont leave. They start talking and share a bit of themselves. During this time, Beauty brings up her feelings of feeling captive by the rules set in place to keep her safe. This is unthinkable to the NS because they were kept captive for so long. She tells Shadow how lonely she is and would like for someone to hold her and sleep with her in their arms. While the storm still rages outside, Shadow decides he'll give her the night in his arm (it's only platonic though). The next morning they're found as they're waking up together and (since being alone with her is really against the rules) Shadow has to go with Security and account for his actions. Breeze goes to talk to Beauty and finds out what happened and also Beauty's need for more than she's allowed by the rules around her. Breeze brings this issue to the attention of the NS leaders and they decide that Beauty and Shadow should spend some time together. <br /><br />Shadow and Beauty are given a chance to bond by being sent to Reservation (another NS compound) and they have 2 weeks together in a secluded cabin. Beauty is interested in Shadow but is very shy and wont make the first move. Shadow at first is rather pissed that they sent him there without actually asking him but does finally admit his return interest in Beauty. The problem lies in the fact that Shadow doesn't know a lot about females and because of what he was put through in the lab, he's afraid he might hurt Beauty if he does try to share sex with her. Things don't go well at first but eventually Beauty takes the bull by the horns and get them talking, which eventually leads to other things...thing that work out very well between them. There are a few stumbling blocks but everything starts going pretty well between Beauty and Shadow. Things get disrupted when mercenaries manage to get on to Reservation, hired by Beauty's previous captor and sent to bring her back to him. They cause a lot of problems but things do get handled and Beauty shows some real courage in handling herself and not being the weak female they all thought her. There's a little stress at the end until Shadow and Beauty are able to talk things out after the danger has been handled and all but they do talk (Beauty showing more courage in not being afraid to speak up for what she wants) and decide they want to stay together. They become mates and start their well deserved HEA.<br /><br />This was a really good story. I loved Beauty and Shadow and seeing them work through their pasts to be together. It was a very good romance but I also liked the story it told about Beauty overcoming how she's seen, both by others and herself, striving to be more and showing a lot of courage when facing danger (both physical and emotional). Shadow did well too but I felt Beauty handled it better than Shadow overall. LOL. I can't wait for book #10, Moon's book (I &lt;3 Moon). I'd recommend this book. 2 thumbs up! :D<br /><br />* note - I listened to the audio version of this book. The narrator did a very good job.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5214641116458096892" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_598218907" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title=" ♥ Rebecca ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/703854-rebecca"><img alt=" ♥ Rebecca ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529467844p2/703854.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" ♥ Rebecca ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" ♥ Rebecca ♥" href="/user/show/703854-rebecca"> ♥ Rebecca ♥</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=sci-fi">sci-fi</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer598218907" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15285043406279547534">I loved this book! I definitely enjoyed it more than <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13107666.Tiger__New_Species___7_' title='Tiger (New Species, #7) by Laurann Dohner' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tiger</a>, and possibly even more tha <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12961307.Justice__New_Species___4_' title='Justice (New Species, #4) by Laurann Dohner' rel='nofollow noopener'>Justice</a>. So the best, or second best of the series so far. At first, I thought people would try to give them a hard time because she is a Gift. But after that initial mix up, once Beauty told Breeze that she was actually interested in Shadow, everyone did everything possible to help make it work for them. They gave Beauty and Shadow all the time and space they needed to get to know each other. It was so easy f</span>
  <span id="freeText15285043406279547534" style="display:none">I loved this book! I definitely enjoyed it more than <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13107666.Tiger__New_Species___7_" title="Tiger (New Species, #7) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Tiger</a>, and possibly even more tha <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12961307.Justice__New_Species___4_" title="Justice (New Species, #4) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Justice</a>. So the best, or second best of the series so far. At first, I thought people would try to give them a hard time because she is a Gift. But after that initial mix up, once Beauty told Breeze that she was actually interested in Shadow, everyone did everything possible to help make it work for them. They gave Beauty and Shadow all the time and space they needed to get to know each other. It was so easy for them. I really dont like when pointless complications get between a couple. Thats why I didnt enjoy <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13107655.Brawn__New_Species___5_" title="Brawn (New Species, #5) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Brawn</a> as much as most, and why I usually dont enjoy contemporary romances. <br /><br />Everything just clicked for Beauty and Shadow. They were amazing and both damaged and adorable with each other. And I <i>loved</i> Beauty. Definitely the best heroine so far. She was Gift, so she was naturally meek and afraid. But you cant have courage without fear, and Beauty definitely has courage. I love how she was able to stand up for herself, unlike the other Gifts, and she even fought for Shadow when she had to. The book still managed to fit in an attempted kidnapping and Beauty handled herself amazingly. Just the right amount of action for this story.<br /><br />There wasnt as much smut-content in this one as the other books. They had sex I think twice before the kidnapping, and once after, which really isnt a lot compared to the rest of the series. But <i>holy eff!</i> They did a 69! I thought, "No way, Laurann isnt gonna go there. Its gonna cut out on us any second now. She's not really gonna go there. Oh my gosh did that just happen?!" I have never seen that done in a book before!<br /><br />I am so excited to read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16005363.Moon__New_Species___10_" title="Moon (New Species, #10) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Moon</a>, but also really sad. Its a lot of fun to marathon a series while it lasts, but when its done its heartbreaking. I dont want it to end, and I am considering checking out one of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/3190846.Laurann_Dohner" title="Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Laurann Dohner</a> other series, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7203997.Ral_s_Woman__Zorn_Warriors___1_" title="Ral's Woman (Zorn Warriors, #1) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Ral's Woman</a> or <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7838460.Burning_up_Flint__Cyborg_Seduction___1_" title="Burning up Flint (Cyborg Seduction, #1) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Burning up Flint</a>, but New Species is her most highly rated.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15285043406279547534" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3123360083" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3123360083" />
    <a title="Elena" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/39044849-elena"><img alt="Elena" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1454369637p2/39044849.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3123360083?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elena" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elena" href="/user/show/39044849-elena">Elena</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39044849-elena?shelf=mf">mf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39044849-elena?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39044849-elena?shelf=hurt-comfort">hurt-comfort</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39044849-elena?shelf=sweet-or-made-me-smile">sweet-or-made-me-smile</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39044849-elena?shelf=fantasy-au-paranormal">fantasy-au-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39044849-elena?shelf=law-police-fire-army-pi">law-police-fire-army-pi</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39044849-elena?shelf=slaves-captives-prisoners-convicts">slaves-captives-prisoners-convicts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39044849-elena?shelf=merfolk-and-other-strange-beings">merfolk-and-other-strange-beings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3123360083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1169344026836953165">3.5 stars!<br/><br/>I'm so glad I've skipped 2 books to read <b>Shadow and Beauty</b>'s story just now! :)<br/><br/>As I assumed, <b>Shadow</b> was sweet and protective of the Gift Female and his awkwardness and insecurities made him even cuter ;)<br/><br/>I loved it that a Gift Female got a book of her own! At last! <b>Beauty</b>, formerly Mud, was imprisoned and abused all her life, so, after freeing her, everyone in NSO assumed she was afraid of all and any males and separated her completely...<br/>She spent her time mostly with Tiny and Halfpint,</span>
  <span id="freeText1169344026836953165" style="display:none">3.5 stars!<br /><br />I'm so glad I've skipped 2 books to read <b>Shadow and Beauty</b>'s story just now! :)<br /><br />As I assumed, <b>Shadow</b> was sweet and protective of the Gift Female and his awkwardness and insecurities made him even cuter ;)<br /><br />I loved it that a Gift Female got a book of her own! At last! <b>Beauty</b>, formerly Mud, was imprisoned and abused all her life, so, after freeing her, everyone in NSO assumed she was afraid of all and any males and separated her completely...<br />She spent her time mostly with Tiny and Halfpint, but also with Breeze. And she simply got curious... about males, about other Species females inviting males to their bedrooms, about the sex itself.<br /><br />It was refreshing to finally see a Species/Species pairing - don't get me wrong, all those big buff NSO officers finding their human mates were so much fun! I simply wanted something new, something fresh and something to show me that those most fragile Species women had 'balls', too... ;)<br /><br /><b>Shadow</b> was great and supportive of <b>Wrath and Lauren</b> already in book 6 of the series, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13107661.Wrath__New_Species___6_" title="Wrath (New Species, #6) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Wrath</a>, and I simply couldn't wait to read his story. And I loved it! :) He's so damaged inside and yet willing to try being with Beauty because she wanted him and to experiment with the big Species in the bedroom.<br /><br />Although not my favourite (I think <b>Wrath</b>'s story is the best so far), I greatly enjoyed this read. Shadow is a great MC, sweet and protective, but also open to new things and respecting Beauty as a Species. And Beauty was simply amazing: curious, brave, fierce (she surprised me with her determination to defend herself and her close ones) - truly, bravo to Ms Dohner for making her a heroine! :)</span>
  <a data-text-id="1169344026836953165" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer10884397333161873898"><strong>Find comfort together</strong><br/><br/>I am so happy that the author told this story. I was really hoping that one of the gift females would find their HEA. The author couldn’t have picked a better mate for Shadow or Beauty, both of them had been through so much. It’s a shame that they had to suffer a few set backs before they found their happiness. I think the author did a fantastic job with this book and I can’t wait to read the next one. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer18281854024251569847"><p>This is one beautiful heart-wrenching story for me. It was something different, something fresh. A different perspective. And most importantly, I get to know a little more about Gift.<br/><br/>Gift are Species but their genetic engineering was that they were created as docile, meek, and submissive. They were ‘domesticated’. They are small, more human in features, and viewed as fragile.   <span id="freeText18281854024251569847" style="display:none"><p>This is one beautiful heart-wrenching story for me. It was something different, something fresh. A different perspective. And most importantly, I get to know a little more about Gift.<br><br>Gift are Species but their genetic engineering was that they were created as docile, meek, and submissive. They were ‘domesticated’. They are small, more human in features, and viewed as fragile. They were specifically created to be given as gift, thus the name, and given to Mercile investors who treated them like pets and sex slaves. Some of them were also sold to the highest bidder.<br><br>Mud was a Gift, rescued from her Master. After the rescue, she took the name Beauty. Freedom didn’t suit well for her. Since they are viewed as fragile, male Species gave a wide berth to them, not approaching because they might bolt, or worse, relive their captivity. But Beauty was not like any other Gift. Her captivity was not any less nightmarish than the others, but she doesn’t cringe and feels afraid if males were to ever approach her. She feels longing, wishing for a connection to another Species.<br><br>Shadow is tainted and fears sex. He suffered under the breeding drugs, and it was the worst that they could have endure, so much worse than the beatings they receive. He fears physical connection because he was afraid to relive what he endured.<br><br>Shadow and Beauty was like a match made from the beginning. That’s all I can think about. And I actually like how they met. I mean, seriously. Tackling someone to the ground under the rain? Yep.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441160680ra/16071864.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My heart aches for the both of them. I wanted them to have their <b>Happily Ever After</b>. It was, for me like a <b>Beauty and the Beast</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441160680ra/16071865.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1441160680ra/16071866.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1440651666ra/16005752.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></p><br></span>

<div id="review_686367390" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/686367390" />
    <a title="PJ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/764355-pj"><img alt="PJ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1413476638p2/764355.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/686367390?book_show_action=true">Aug 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="PJ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="PJ" href="/user/show/764355-pj">PJ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/764355-pj?shelf=2013-books-i-ve-read">2013-books-i-ve-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/764355-pj?shelf=romance-alpha-male">romance-alpha-male</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer686367390" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17362627585486521590">I absolutely loved Laurann Dohner's New Species series! That said Shadow and Beauty's story was my least favorite. It's not that I didn't like it, it just didn't hold my interest as much. Still, it shouldn't be skipped, as it builds up the tension to Moon, the last story, so far, in the New Species series. And Moon may just be my favorite.<br/><br/>I definitely recommend the NS series to paranormal-rom fans: the Males are hot and strong and speak English as if it's their second language and the human fema</span>
  <span id="freeText17362627585486521590" style="display:none">I absolutely loved Laurann Dohner's New Species series! That said Shadow and Beauty's story was my least favorite. It's not that I didn't like it, it just didn't hold my interest as much. Still, it shouldn't be skipped, as it builds up the tension to Moon, the last story, so far, in the New Species series. And Moon may just be my favorite.<br /><br />I definitely recommend the NS series to paranormal-rom fans: the Males are hot and strong and speak English as if it's their second language and the human females who pursue them are tough, feisty and go after what they want. Even little Beauty, a NS Gift Female, although she's more mousy about it. <br /><br />There's lots of humor, passion, snarls and roars as human genes mixed with canine, feline and primate DNA make for some buff and tough males. Mix in human females, who gasp at their first glimpse of NS males and things get HOT fast! There's a light-heartedness and childlike curiosity that's very appealing. It pokes fun at humans and our obsessive, controlling nature. Best of all, once Males choose a Mate they bond for life and practically gag at any other women's scent. Yep, that's zero chance of cheating, a comfort to most.<br /><br />Lastly, I strongly urge you to read this series in order. They can be read as stand-alones, but the background stories definitely grow and weave together as the New Species find their way in our word and bond as a community finally free to build their own brand new Homeland.<br /><br />Recommend: Romance Fans Yes / Paranormal Nerds BIG YES!<br />Reread: Yes, I'll definitely reread my favorites, which is most of them.<br />Steam: Constant Simmer to Roiling Boil <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17362627585486521590" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_312482589" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/312482589" />
    <a title="Shannon (Savhage Temptrest)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2524324-shannon-savhage-temptrest"><img alt="Shannon (Savhage Temptrest)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1321085577p2/2524324.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/312482589?book_show_action=true">Apr 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon (Savhage Temptrest)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon (Savhage Temptrest)" href="/user/show/2524324-shannon-savhage-temptrest">Shannon (Savhage Temptrest)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer312482589" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16886849175003838943">Laurann Dohner has done it again with this kick-a$$ novel based in her New Species series.<br/><br/>We finally get a love story between two New Species as all the males usually prefer human women and the female New Species normally don't want to settle down. Enter Shadow, a New Species male who is on the outskirts of his new found civilization and who is haunted by his past in the Mercile labs, and then there is Beauty, a New Species Gift female who's own past captivity with her "master" has left her lone</span>
  <span id="freeText16886849175003838943" style="display:none">Laurann Dohner has done it again with this kick-a$$ novel based in her New Species series.<br /><br />We finally get a love story between two New Species as all the males usually prefer human women and the female New Species normally don't want to settle down. Enter Shadow, a New Species male who is on the outskirts of his new found civilization and who is haunted by his past in the Mercile labs, and then there is Beauty, a New Species Gift female who's own past captivity with her "master" has left her lonely and trying desperately to adjust to this new life and "freedom."<br /><br />These two just totally worked for me with their passion and their emotional issues. I loved that both Shadow and Beauty laid their vulnerabilities on the table and kept their budding romance filled with honesty and hope. <br /><br />I personally love the whole "alpha male" character because while they can be pushy the emotions and backstory shines through and makes me sigh with envy for their lucky heroines! Although the ebook I purchased needed a more thorough edit, this story has truly reminded me why I love to read Laurann Dohner books! Definitely recommended for fans of the series and erotic, paranormal romance novels in general!</span>
  <a data-text-id="16886849175003838943" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText13343235461431148669" style="display:none">4 Shadow Stars <br /><br />This book was a little different than what we are used to. <br />Beauty is Species but she is also a gifted female. Meaning she was made smaller almost helpless and sold to sick people who wanted to “own” a pet. <br /><br />Sick right! I was glad when this one was saved in a previous book. But Beauty wants to be more like the other Females, but because she is a gift all her people protect her even from themselves. <br /><br />She is very attracted to Shadow and Shadow is very attracted to her but because she is labeled gift he stays away. <br /><br />But the heart wants and even when they are put together. I was so saddened to see how much they both “hide” there true feelings because of there pasts.<br /><br />They kind of heal each other. I enjoyed this book a lot. It was different and we get to see a different kind of love story. And how pain can heal pain. <br /><br />Again the narration blows me away. Vanessa does a fabulous job as always.<br /><br />*You don't have to like my review but its 100% my opinion, and I am allowed to have it.*</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1570360541777560300">Shadow is the newest installment in the New Species world. I fall in love (and in some cases, lust) with all of the hereos in this series. They all have an irresistable quality, different for each male, that makes every one of them vulnerable in some way.<br/>This book opens with what happens in the van after Beauty is rescued in Justice's book, and then jumps right into the story line. There is a beautiful, but heartbreaking, innocence for both Shadow and Beauty in this book (even though both are vi</span>
  <span id="freeText1570360541777560300" style="display:none">Shadow is the newest installment in the New Species world. I fall in love (and in some cases, lust) with all of the hereos in this series. They all have an irresistable quality, different for each male, that makes every one of them vulnerable in some way.<br />This book opens with what happens in the van after Beauty is rescued in Justice's book, and then jumps right into the story line. There is a beautiful, but heartbreaking, innocence for both Shadow and Beauty in this book (even though both are victims of sexual abuse) that Ms. Dohner handles well.<br />Shadow is light on the sex that the other books have in abundance, and it makes for a better story considering the issues both characters have to work through.</span>

  <span id="freeText13611162402959473983" style="display:none"><b>Shadow...<br>A person who is only cool because of his name. <br>3 Stars for your time to shine in this series!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1486442349ra/21914557.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13566041.Shadow__New_Species___9_" title="Shadow (New Species, #9) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Shadow</a> is my least favorite book of the bunch.<br>Maybe other people liked this, but in truth, it was pretty bland compared to other installments in this series.<br>This is the story of SHADOW and his Beauty... Love the name! The guy, not so much. <br>I can't help repeating it. Shadow... Shadow...</i><br><b><br>So we meet Shadow in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13107661.Wrath__New_Species___6_" title="Wrath (New Species, #6) by Laurann Dohner" rel="nofollow noopener">Wrath</a>, the 6th book in the series.<br>Now he is a guard at Homeland. In a stormy night, he meets our heroine, a primate Gift named Beauty. <br>Gifts are more fragile than Species. They were engineered by Mercile to be pretty, tamed and usable like pets or worse! Homeland has certain protocols for them and rules. They do their best to shelter and overprotect them.<br>Despite her unfortunate past, Beauty wants to be different and decides to take the reigns of her own life. </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1555840926ra/27392552.gif" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>It wilts in comparison to other stories that I truly love.<br>The romance is sweet and they make a cute couple, but that's pretty much it.<br>I liked Beauty a lot and enjoyed how she matures, how she fights for what she wants. Shadow was a cool guy. He was OK in my list of hot studs. Still, their relationship and hardships didn't move my heart. It just seemed dull, not bad, just dull.<br><br>The writing and pace were ok. And it's not that I didn't enjoy it... I guess it didn't make an impact on me. It's different, but not in a good or bad way. </i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1555851108i/27393747._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>So... I wouldn't qualify it as a waste of time. Many readers seemed to love this one, but I disagree strongly. <br>I feel the need to say that maybe this is the only one I might have skipped. To summarize this cocktail of thoughts, this was not a memorable read. Entertaining enough to finish but not enough to win more than a 3. <br>I bid you farewell and may your reads be fab!</b></span>

<div id="review_363845483" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/363845483" />
    <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog"><img alt="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352609417p2/2489554.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/363845483?book_show_action=true">Jul 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)" href="/user/show/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog">Annie (Under the Covers Book Blog)</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=review-requests">review-requests</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=pnr">pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-laurann-dohner">author-laurann-dohner</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2489554-annie-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=series-new-species">series-new-species</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer363845483" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15173350658980689468">3.5 stars<br/><br/><b> Posted on<a href='http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2012/11/review-shadow-by-laurann-dohner.html' rel='nofollow noopener'> Under the Covers</a></b><br/><br/>Beauty is a Gift, which means that she is treated with the utmost respect and reverence. Many give her a wide berth because they know of her traumatic past. As a survivor of a brutal captivity, Beauty shows her strength in a way that is quiet, but very much noticeable and admirable. I really liked Beauty’s character because even though she is scared beyond her wits, she is still able to keep her head on straight. I loved the way she was able to stand up to cer</span>
  <span id="freeText15173350658980689468" style="display:none">3.5 stars<br /><br /><b> Posted on<a href="http://www.underthecoversbookblog.com/2012/11/review-shadow-by-laurann-dohner.html" rel="nofollow noopener"> Under the Covers</a></b><br /><br />Beauty is a Gift, which means that she is treated with the utmost respect and reverence. Many give her a wide berth because they know of her traumatic past. As a survivor of a brutal captivity, Beauty shows her strength in a way that is quiet, but very much noticeable and admirable. I really liked Beauty’s character because even though she is scared beyond her wits, she is still able to keep her head on straight. I loved the way she was able to stand up to certain people when they simply judged her wrongly. Despite the fact that she was a victim, she doesn’t allow that to simply run her life anymore.<br /><br />Shadow is the New Species male who is now protecting her. After spending one night lying next to her during a storm Shadow and Beauty share an unbreakable bond now that Dohner takes and builds upon that.<br /><br />Though slower in pacing, I found that I enjoyed several elements of this book, the budding romance between Beauty and Shadow my favorite. The one thing that dropped this book down from a solid four star rating was simply the pacing. Some scenes dragged on for too long for me and I think it impeded the natural progression of the story. Also, I felt like there was less action than the book prior to this.<br /><br />*Review copy provided by publisher</span>
  <a data-text-id="15173350658980689468" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_440102827" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/440102827" />
    <a title="♆ BookAddict  ✒ La Crimson Femme" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3089655-bookaddict-la-crimson-femme"><img alt="♆ BookAddict  ✒ La Crimson Femme" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1537761015p2/3089655.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/440102827?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♆ BookAddict  ✒ La Crimson Femme" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♆ BookAddict  ✒ La Crimson Femme" href="/user/show/3089655-bookaddict-la-crimson-femme">♆ BookAddict  ✒ La Crimson Femme</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/18866287-shadow">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Paranormal Romance lovers</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3089655-bookaddict-la-crimson-femme?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3089655-bookaddict-la-crimson-femme?shelf=z-nlg">z-nlg</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3089655-bookaddict-la-crimson-femme?shelf=parahuman">parahuman</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer440102827" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9087288006069028243">Finally a story with a Gifted female with a New Species male. Beauty is a primate and easily mistaken as a human. She's right that she's still being treated like a prisoner even though she's been freed. I'm a bit startled how much they wrap her up in bubble wrap. It's a bit depressing. She's pissed about it and I can totally understand it. Who wouldn't be pissed being treated like a stupid child?<br/><br/>Fortunately, Shadow doesn't think she's a stupid child. He is hesitant but good think for Beauty. She</span>
  <span id="freeText9087288006069028243" style="display:none">Finally a story with a Gifted female with a New Species male. Beauty is a primate and easily mistaken as a human. She's right that she's still being treated like a prisoner even though she's been freed. I'm a bit startled how much they wrap her up in bubble wrap. It's a bit depressing. She's pissed about it and I can totally understand it. Who wouldn't be pissed being treated like a stupid child?<br /><br />Fortunately, Shadow doesn't think she's a stupid child. He is hesitant but good think for Beauty. She convinces him otherwise. I did like the little phrase from Breeze - "gift wrapped" That was hilarious. I approve. <br /><br />This story is the second one which doesn't include the "hater" group. I am thankful for it being missed. We can focus on the sweet romance between two damaged Species. It's a lovely thing to see them overcome their rape and be able to enjoy each other. Learning more about the drug company and the Gifted females enhanced the story. I'm hoping we get to have a story about Moon next. I'm worried about Moon. I love that name.<br /><br />Overall, this story was sweet and predictable. It's a good happily ever after romance which I can recommend to paranormal romance lovers.</span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('obh51Nx4bVGIlE4WZ3n6T1TiEFqGXSb8PQzcIESMaPkldx/QpruE79noMfLNQR04EklDorniVbOhT8f8MJBafQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('SXtQG2JLG3Z8ELbhcwqTWkBpbqHTIkFcY+84ksdgGoDNtDYfGIjyyC1syQXZMnQtBsI9WeydMhP/rCNOs3woBA==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6676715015446272102">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've alw</span>
  <span id="freeText6676715015446272102" style="display:none">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've always been a daydreamer, and I'm a HUGE fan of books, always have been.<br /><br />No, I didn't know that I always wanted to write. I inhaled books as a child. I read entire series (Pippi Longstocking, Nancy Drew and The Hardy Boys, Trixie Beldon, The Borrowers, etc) in a matter of days at a time. By the time I was nine years old I had an adult library card where I visited often. I moved on to John Saul, Stephen King, Richard Laymon, Agatha Christie, and then found romance. I was hooked. I wrote poetry in my teens and then moved on to short stories. My first book was started after I read a real bomb of a book that ticked me off with really horrible characters and a plot that was shabby at best and I thought... I could do better. LOL.<br /><br />I wrote my first book which will probably never see the light of day in the early 90's. I wrote a series of a few books from it. I'm a series fan! I kept writing for fun, wrote MANY books and then in 2009 I decided to try to get published. I wrote my first Sci Fi romance and Ral's Woman came to be. I submitted it and with a little tweaking, Ellorascave sent me an acceptance letter. It was kind of a 'Cinderella' experience for me. It's been a terrific ride so far and I'm really happy that I finally had the time to commit to writing full time. It's a dream come true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="6676715015446272102" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
